04/08/23, 5:19 pm - angraj dewangan: Types of Insurance:

Life Insurance: Provides financial protection to the insured's beneficiaries in the event of the policyholder's death. It offers various plans like term, whole life, and endowment policies.
Non-life (General) Insurance: Covers assets and liabilities against risks other than death, such as health, property, motor, travel, and marine insurance.
Features and Needs:

Life Insurance Features: Pays a death benefit, offers tax benefits, savings component, and provides financial security to the family.
Non-life Insurance Features: Provides coverage for specific risks and damages, tailored to the insured's needs.
Needs for Life Insurance: Financial security for dependents, debt repayment, wealth accumulation, and retirement planning.
Needs for Non-life Insurance: Protection against unexpected events, asset protection, and compliance with legal requirements.
Policies of Different Types of Insurance:
Each type of insurance has specific policies that outline the terms and conditions of coverage, premium payments, and claim procedures.

Control of Malpractices and Miss Sell:
Regulatory bodies and laws are in place to monitor insurance practices and prevent malpractices, ensuring fair and transparent transactions.

Negligence, Loss Assessment, and Loss Control:
Insured parties are required to take reasonable care to prevent loss or damage. Loss assessment is the process of evaluating the extent of the loss, and loss control involves measures to minimize risks.

Computation of Insurance Premium:
Premiums are calculated based on various factors like the type of insurance, coverage amount, age, health status, occupation, and risk profile of the insured.

Dematerialization of Insurance Policies:
Dematerialization is the process of converting physical insurance policies into electronic form, enhancing accessibility and reducing the risk of policy loss.

Claims and Settlement Procedure:
When a loss occurs, the insured can file a claim with the insurance company. The company then evaluates the claim and, if approved, settles the amount as per the terms of the policy.

Please note that these are brief notes, and each topic can be further expanded with more details and examples. Let me know if you need any specific information or have further questions!
